<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">

<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Hôtellerie - Hôpital Saint-Jean</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>

<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #e67e22;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-hotel"></i> Service hôtellerie</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='index.html'">Accueil</button>
        </div>
    </nav>
    <div class="container-fluid px-4 mt-3">
        <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="window.location.href='ajout-chambre.html'">
            <i class="fas fa-plus"></i> Nouvelle chambre
        </button>
        <button class="btn btn-primary ms-2" onclick="window.location.href='ajout-commande.html'">
            <i class="fas fa-plus"></i> Nouvelle commande
        </button>
    </div>

    <div class="container-fluid px-4 py-4">
        <h2>Occupation des chambres</h2>
        <div id="chambresList" class="loading-container mt-4">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Chargement des chambres...</p>
        </div>

        <h2 class="mt-5">Commandes repas</h2>
        <div id="commandesList" class="loading-container mt-4">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Chargement des commandes...</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        (async function () {
            try {
                // Chambres
                const chambres = await API.get('/chambres');
                const chambresContainer = document.getElementById('chambresList');
                if (chambres.length) {
                    chambresContainer.innerHTML = chambres.map(c => `
                        <div class="consultation-card mb-2" style="border-left-color: #e67e22;">
                            <strong>Chambre ${c.numero}</strong> (${c.type})<br>
                            Capacité : ${c.capacite} personne(s)<br>
                            Statut : <span class="badge-custom badge-${c.statut === 'libre' ? 'success' : c.statut === 'occupee' ? 'info' : 'warning'}">${c.statut}</span>
                        </div>
                    `).join('');
                } else {
                    chambresContainer.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucune chambre trouvée.</p>';
                }

                // Commandes repas
                const commandes = await API.get('/commandes');
                const commandesContainer = document.getElementById('commandesList');
                if (commandes.length) {
                    commandesContainer.innerHTML = commandes.map(cmd => `
                        <div class="consultation-card mb-2" style="border-left-color: #e67e22;">
                            <strong>Patient : ${cmd.nom} ${cmd.prenom}</strong><br>
                            Service : ${cmd.type_service}<br>
                            Statut : <span class="badge-custom badge-${cmd.statut === 'livre' ? 'success' : cmd.statut === 'pret' ? 'info' : 'warning'}">${cmd.statut}</span>
                        </div>
                    `).join('');
                } else {
                    commandesContainer.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucune commande trouvée.</p>';
                }

            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('chambresList').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger">Erreur chargement.</p>';
            }
        })();
    </script>
</body>

</html>

    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
    <script src="https://unpkg.com/aos@2.3.1/dist/aos.js"></script>

    <script>
        AOS.init({ duration: 1000 });

        window.addEventListener('scroll', function () {
            const navbar = document.querySelector('.navbar');
            if (window.scrollY > 50) {
                navbar.classList.add('scrolled');
            } else {
                navbar.classList.remove('scrolled');
            }
        });

        function selectProfil(profil, element) {
            document.querySelectorAll('.profil-option').forEach(opt => opt.classList.remove('selected'));
            element.classList.add('selected');
            document.getElementById('profil-select').value = profil;
        }

        function login() {
            const profil = document.getElementById('profil-select').value;
            const username = document.getElementById('username').value;
            const password = document.getElementById('password').value;

            const redirections = {
                'medecin': 'dashboard-medecin.html',
                'infirmier': 'dashboard-infirmier.html',
                'direction': 'dashboard-direction.html',
                'administratif': 'dashboard-admin.html',
                'hotellerie': 'hotellerie.html',
                'logistique': 'stocks.html',
                'qualite': 'qualite.html',
                'voyages': 'voyages.html'
            };

            window.location.href = redirections[profil];
        }
    </script>
</body>

    <div class="inscription-container">
        <div class="header">
            <i class="fab fa-whatsapp"></i>

        </div>

        <div class="body">
            <div id="successAlert" class="alert alert-success"></div>
            <div id="errorAlert" class="alert alert-danger"></div>

            <div class="phone-display">
                <i class="fas fa-phone-alt me-2"></i>
                Numéro vérifié :
                <span id="displayPhone">Chargement...</span>
            </div>

            <form id="inscriptionForm">
                <div class="row">
                    <div class="col-md-6">
                        <input type="text" class="form-control" id="nom" placeholder="Nom" required>
                    </div>

                    </div>
                </div>

                <input type="text" class="form-control" id="adresse" placeholder="Adresse" required>

                <select class="form-control" id="groupeSanguin">
                    <option value="">Groupe sanguin</option>
                    <option>A+</option>
                    <option>A-</option>
                    <option>B+</option>
                    <option>B-</option>
                    <option>AB+</option>
                    <option>AB-</option>
                    <option>O+</option>
                    <option>O-</option>
                </select>

                <input type="text" class="form-control" id="allergies" placeholder="Allergies (optionnel)">

                <button type="submit" class="btn-inscription" id="submitBtn">
                    <i class="fas fa-check-circle me-2"></i>
                    Créer mon compte
                </button>

                <div id="spinner" class="spinner"></div>
            </form>

            <div class="text-center mt-3">
                <a href="connexion-whatsapp.html" class="text-decoration-none">
                    <i class="fas fa-arrow-left me-2"></i>
                    Retour
                </a>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        
    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const telephone = urlParams.get('tel');
    const tempToken = urlParams.get('token');

    document.getElementById('displayPhone').textContent = telephone || 'Numéro inconnu';

    function showSuccess(message) {
        const alert = document.getElementById('successAlert');
        alert.textContent = message;
        alert.style.display = 'block';
        setTimeout(() => alert.style.display = 'none', 3000);
    }

    function showError(message) {
        const alert = document.getElementById('errorAlert');
        alert.textContent = message;
        alert.style.display = 'block';
        setTimeout(() => alert.style.display = 'none', 3000);
    }

    function showLoading(show) {
        document.getElementById('spinner').style.display = show ? 'block' : 'none';
        document.getElementById('submitBtn').disabled = show;
    }

    document.getElementById('inscriptionForm').addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();

        const formData = {
            telephone: telephone,
            whatsapp: telephone,
            nom: document.getElementById('nom').value,
            prenom: document.getElementById('prenom').value,
            date_naissance: document.getElementById('dateNaissance').value,
            email: document.getElementById('email').value,
            adresse: document.getElementById('adresse').value,
            groupe_sanguin: document.getElementById('groupeSanguin').value,
            allergies: document.getElementById('allergies').value || 'Aucune',
            type: 'patient'
        };

        showLoading(true);

        try {
            const response = await fetch('https://clinique-hoteliere-et-actions.onrender.com/api/beneficiaires', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${tempToken}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(formData)
            });

            const data = await response.json();

            if (response.ok) {
                localStorage.setItem('token', data.token);
                console.log('Token stocké :', data.token);
                showSuccess('✅ Inscription réussie !');
                setTimeout(() => {
                    window.location.href = 'dashboard-patient.html';
                }, 2000);
            } else {
                showError(data.error || 'Erreur lors de l\'inscription');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erreur réseau :', error);
            showError('Erreur de connexion');
        } finally {
            showLoading(false);
        }
    });
    </script>
</body>

</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Mes rendez-vous - Hôpital Saint-Jean</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>
<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #3498db;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-calendar-check"></i> Mes rendez-vous</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='dashboard-patient.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container-fluid px-4 py-4">
        <h2>Vos rendez-vous</h2>
        <div id="rdvList" class="loading-container mt-4">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Chargement de vos rendez-vous...</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        async function chargerRdv() {
            const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
            if (!token) {
                window.location.href = 'index.html';
                return;
            }

            const payload = JSON.parse(atob(token.split('.')[1]));
            const id_beneficiaire = payload.id;

            try {
                const rdvs = await API.get('/rendez-vous');
                const container = document.getElementById('rdvList');

                // Filtrer les rendez-vous du patient connecté
                const mesRdvs = rdvs.filter(r => r.id_beneficiaire === id_beneficiaire);

                if (mesRdvs.length) {
                    container.innerHTML = mesRdvs.map(r => `
                        <div class="consultation-card mb-2">
                            <strong>${new Date(r.date_rdv).toLocaleDateString('fr-FR')} à ${new Date(r.date_rdv).toLocaleTimeString('fr-FR', {hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit'})}</strong><br>
                            Motif : ${r.motif || 'Non précisé'}<br>
                            Statut : <span class="badge-custom badge-${r.statut === 'confirmé' ? 'success' : 'warning'}">${r.statut}</span>
                        </div>
                    `).join('');
                } else {
                    container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucun rendez-vous trouvé.</p>';
                }
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('rdvList').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger">Erreur chargement.</p>';
            }
        }

        chargerRdv();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>
<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #3498db;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-envelope"></i> Mes messages</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='dashboard-patient.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container-fluid px-4 py-4">
        <h2>Votre messagerie</h2>
        <div id="messagesContainer" class="loading-container mt-4">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Chargement de vos messages...</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        function chargerMessages() {
            console.log('chargerMessages() exécuté');
            const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
            if (!token) {
                return;
            }

            // Simuler des messages
            const messages = [
                { expediteur: "Dr. Diallo", date: "19/03/2026", contenu: "Vos résultats d'analyse sont disponibles.", lu: false },
                { expediteur: "Secrétariat", date: "18/03/2026", contenu: "Rappel : rendez-vous le 25/03 à 09h30.", lu: true },
                { expediteur: "Service facturation", date: "17/03/2026", contenu: "Votre facture du 10/03 est disponible.", lu: true }
            ];

            const container = document.getElementById('messagesContainer');
            if (messages.length) {
                container.innerHTML = messages.map(m => `
                    <div class="consultation-card mb-2 ${!m.lu ? 'unread' : ''}">
                        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between">
                            <strong>${m.expediteur}</strong>
                            <small class="text-muted">${m.date}</small>
                        </div>
                        <p class="mb-1">${m.contenu}</p>
                        ${!m.lu ? '<span class="badge-custom badge-info">Nouveau</span>' : ''}
                    </div>
                `).join('');
            } else {
                container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucun message.</p>';
            }
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', chargerMessages);
    </script>
</body>
</html>

        (async function () {

                const params = await API.get('/parametres');
                const container = document.getElementById('parametresContainer');
                if (params.length) {
                    // Grouper par catégories (simulées)
                    const etablissement = params.filter(p => ['nom_etablissement', 'adresse', 'telephone'].includes(p.cle));
                    const preferences = params.filter(p => ['langue', 'fuseau_horaire'].includes(p.cle));

                    container.innerHTML = `
                        <div class="col-md-6">
                            <div class="card-custom">
                                <h5>Établissement</h5>
                                ${etablissement.map(p => `<p><strong>${p.description} :</strong> ${p.valeur}</p>`).join('')}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="col-md-6">
                            <div class="card-custom">
                                <h5>Préférences</h5>
                                ${preferences.map(p => `<p><strong>${p.description} :</strong> ${p.valeur}</p>`).join('')}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    `;
                } else {
                    container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucun paramètre trouvé.</p>';
                }
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('parametresContainer').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger">Erreur chargement.</p>';
            }
        })();
    </script>
</body>

<script>
    async function chargerSpecialistes() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/specialistes');
            const specialistes = await response.json();
            const container = document.getElementById('specialistesList');
            if (specialistes.length) {
                container.innerHTML = specialistes.map(s => `
                    <div class="col-md-4 mb-4">
                        <div class="card h-100 shadow-sm">
                            <img src="${s.photo_url || 'https://via.placeholder.com/300x200?text=Photo'}" class="card-img-top" alt="Photo de ${s.nom} ${s.prenom}" style="height: 250px; object-fit: cover;">
                            <div class="card-body">
                                <h5 class="card-title">Dr. ${s.nom} ${s.prenom}</h5>
                                <p class="card-text"><strong>Spécialité :</strong> ${s.specialite}</p>
                                <p class="card-text"><strong>Tél :</strong> ${s.telephone || 'Non renseigné'}</p>
                                <p class="card-text"><strong>Email :</strong> ${s.email || 'Non renseigné'}</p>
                                <p class="card-text">${s.description || ''}</p>
                                ${s.cv_url ? `<a href="${s.cv_url}" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" target="_blank">Voir le CV</a>` : ''}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `).join('');
            } else {
                container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-center">Aucun spécialiste trouvé.</p>';
            }
        } catch (e) {
            document.getElementById('specialistesList').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger text-center">Erreur chargement.</p>';
        }
    }
    chargerSpecialistes();
</script>

        (async function () {
            try {
                const produits = await API.get('/produits');
                const container = document.getElementById('stocksList');
                if (produits.length) {
                    container.innerHTML = produits.map(p => {
                        const alerte = p.stock_actuel < p.seuil_alerte;
                        return `
                            <div class="consultation-card mb-2" style="border-left-color: ${alerte ? '#e74c3c' : '#27ae60'};">
                                <strong>${p.nom}</strong><br>
                                Stock : ${p.stock_actuel} (seuil : ${p.seuil_alerte})<br>
                                Type : ${p.type}<br>
                                ${alerte ? '<span class="badge-custom badge-danger">Stock faible</span>' : ''}
                            </div>
                        `;
                    }).join('');
                } else {
                    container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucun produit trouvé.</p>';
                }
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('stocksList').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger">Erreur chargement.</p>';
            }
        })();
    </script>
</body>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">

<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Nouvelle admission</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>

<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #8e44ad;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-user-plus"></i> Nouvelle admission</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='dashboard-admin.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container mt-5">
        <div class="card-custom">
            <h2 class="mb-4">Admettre un patient</h2>
            <form id="admissionForm">
                <div class="mb-3">
                    <label>ID du patient</label>
                    <input type="number" class="form-control" id="id_beneficiaire" required>
                </div>
                <div class="mb-3">
                    <label>Service</label>
                    <input type="text" class="form-control" id="service" required>
                </div>
                <div class="mb-3">
                    <label>Médecin responsable</label>
                    <select class="form-control" id="id_medecin" required>
                        <option value="">Chargement...</option>
                    </select>
                </div>
                <div class="mb-3">
                    <label>Statut</label>
                    <select class="form-control" id="statut">
                        <option value="en_attente">En attente</option>
                        <option value="en_cours">En cours</option>
                        <option value="termine">Terminé</option>
                    </select>
                </div>

                <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary">Enregistrer</button>
            </form>
            <div id="message" class="mt-3"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        async function chargerMedecins() {
            try {
                const medecins = await API.get('/personnel/medecins');
                const select = document.getElementById('id_medecin');
                select.innerHTML = '<option value="">Sélectionner un médecin</option>';
                medecins.forEach(m => {
                    select.innerHTML += `<option value="${m.id_personnel}">Dr. ${m.prenom} ${m.nom}</option>`;
                });
            } catch (e) {
                console.error("Erreur chargement médecins", e);
            }
        }
        chargerMedecins();
        document.getElementById('admissionForm').addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            const data = {
                id_beneficiaire: document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire').value,
                service: document.getElementById('service').value,
                medecin: document.getElementById('id_medecin').value,
                statut: document.getElementById('statut').value
            };
            try {
                const result = await API.post('/admissions', data);
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-success">Admission enregistrée (ID ${result.id})</div>`;
                document.getElementById('admissionForm').reset();
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Erreur lors de l\'admission</div>';
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>

</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">

<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Nouvelle chambre</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>

<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #e67e22;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-door-open"></i> Nouvelle chambre</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='hotellerie.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container mt-5">
        <div class="card-custom">
            <h2 class="mb-4">Ajouter une chambre</h2>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Numéro</label>
                <input type="text" class="form-control" id="numero" required>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Type</label>
                <select class="form-control" id="type">
                    <option value="standard">Standard</option>
                    <option value="medicalisee">Médicalisée</option>
                    <option value="suite">Suite</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Capacité</label>
                <input type="number" class="form-control" id="capacite" value="1" min="1">
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Statut</label>
                <select class="form-control" id="statut">
                    <option value="libre">Libre</option>
                    <option value="occupee">Occupée</option>
                    <option value="maintenance">Maintenance</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <button class="btn btn-success" onclick="enregistrerChambre()">Ajouter</button>
            <div id="message" class="mt-3"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        async function enregistrerChambre() {
            const data = {
                numero: document.getElementById('numero').value,
                type: document.getElementById('type').value,
                capacite: parseInt(document.getElementById('capacite').value), // ✅ conversion en nombre
                statut: document.getElementById('statut').value
            };
            if (!data.numero) {
                return document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-warning">Numéro requis</div>';
            }
            console.log('Données envoyées :', data);
            try {
                const result = await API.post('/chambres', data);
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-success">Chambre ajoutée (ID ${result.id})</div>`;
                document.getElementById('numero').value = '';
                document.getElementById('capacite').value = 1;
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Erreur : ' + e.message + '</div>';
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>

</html>

        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container mt-5">
        <div class="card-custom">
            <h2 class="mb-4">Commander un repas</h2>

            <div class="mb-3">

                    <option value="">Chargement...</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Type de service</label>
                <select class="form-control" id="type_service">
                    <option value="salle">Salle</option>
                    <option value="hospitalisation">Hospitalisation</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Régime</label>
                <input type="text" class="form-control" id="regime" placeholder="ex: Sans sel, diabétique...">
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Instructions</label>
                <textarea class="form-control" id="instructions" rows="2"></textarea>
            </div>

            <button class="btn btn-success" onclick="enregistrerCommande()">Commander</button>
            <div id="message" class="mt-3"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        async function chargerPatients() {
            const patients = await API.get('/beneficiaires');
            const select = document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire');
            select.innerHTML = '<option value="">Choisir un patient</option>';
            patients.forEach(p => {
                select.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id_beneficiaire}">${p.nom} ${p.prenom}</option>`;
            });
        }
        chargerPatients();

        async function enregistrerCommande() {
            const data = {
                id_beneficiaire: document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire').value,
                type_service: document.getElementById('type_service').value,
                regime: document.getElementById('regime').value,
                instructions: document.getElementById('instructions').value
            };
            if (!data.id_beneficiaire) {
                return document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-warning">Patient requis</div>';
            }
            try {
                const result = await API.post('/commandes', data);
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-success">Commande enregistrée (ID ${result.id})</div>`;
                document.getElementById('regime').value = '';
                document.getElementById('instructions').value = '';
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Erreur</div>';
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>

</html>

            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm"
                onclick="window.location.href='dashboard-infirmier.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container mt-5">
        <div class="card-custom">
            <h2 class="mb-4">Enregistrer des constantes</h2>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Patient</label>
                <select class="form-control" id="id_beneficiaire" required>
                    <option value="">Chargement des patients...</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <div class="row">
                <div class="col-md-6 mb-3">
                    <label>Tension artérielle</label>
                    <input type="text" class="form-control" id="tension" placeholder="ex: 120/80">
                </div>
                <div class="col-md-6 mb-3">
                    <label>Pouls (bpm)</label>
                    <input type="number" class="form-control" id="pouls">
                </div>
            </div>

            <div class="row">
                <div class="col-md-6 mb-3">
                    <label>Température (°C)</label>
                    <input type="number" step="0.1" class="form-control" id="temperature">
                </div>
                <div class="col-md-6 mb-3">
                    <label>Saturation O2 (%)</label>
                    <input type="number" class="form-control" id="saturation">
                </div>
            </div>

            <button class="btn btn-success" onclick="enregistrerConstante()">Enregistrer</button>
            <div id="message" class="mt-3"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        async function chargerPatients() {
            try {
                const patients = await API.get('/beneficiaires');
                const select = document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire');
                select.innerHTML = '<option value="">Choisir un patient</option>';
                patients.forEach(p => {
                    select.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id_beneficiaire}">${p.nom} ${p.prenom}</option>`;
                });
            } catch (e) {
                console.error("Erreur chargement patients", e);
            }
        }
        chargerPatients();

        async function enregistrerConstante() {
            const data = {
                id_beneficiaire: document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire').value,
                tension: document.getElementById('tension').value,
                pouls: document.getElementById('pouls').value,
                temperature: document.getElementById('temperature').value,
                saturation: document.getElementById('saturation').value
            };

            if (!data.id_beneficiaire) {
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-warning">Veuillez choisir un patient</div>';
                return;
            }

            try {
                const result = await API.post('/constantes', data);
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-success">Constante enregistrée (ID ${result.id})</div>`;
                document.getElementById('tension').value = '';
                document.getElementById('pouls').value = '';
                document.getElementById('temperature').value = '';
                document.getElementById('saturation').value = '';
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Erreur lors de l\'enregistrement</div>';
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>

</html>

                </div>
                <div class="mb-3">

                    <input type="datetime-local" class="form-control" id="date_heure" required>
                </div>
                <div class="mb-3">
                    <label>Motif</label>
                    <textarea class="form-control" id="motif" rows="2"></textarea>
                </div>
                <div class="mb-3">

                    <select class="form-control" id="type">

                    </select>
                </div>
                <div class="mb-3">
                    <label>Statut</label>
                    <select class="form-control" id="statut">
                        <option value="planifiee">Planifiée</option>
                        <option value="realisee">Réalisée</option>
                        <option value="annulee">Annulée</option>
                    </select>
                </div>
                <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary">Enregistrer</button>
            </form>
            <div id="message" class="mt-3"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        document.getElementById('consultationForm').addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
            e.preventDefault();
            const data = {
                id_beneficiaire: document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire').value,
                id_medecin: document.getElementById('id_medecin').value,
                date_heure: document.getElementById('date_heure').value,
                motif: document.getElementById('motif').value,
                type: document.getElementById('type').value,
                statut: document.getElementById('statut').value
            };
            try {
                const result = await API.post('/consultations', data);
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-success">Consultation ajoutée (ID ${result.id})</div>`;
                document.getElementById('consultationForm').reset();
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Erreur lors de l\'ajout</div>';
            }
        });
    </script>
</body>

</html>

=== FICHIER: ajout-course.html ===
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">

<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Nouvelle course</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>

<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #3498db;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-truck"></i> Nouvelle course</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='voyages.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container mt-5">
        <div class="card-custom">
            <h2 class="mb-4">Planifier un transport</h2>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Véhicule</label>
                <select class="form-control" id="id_vehicule" required>
                    <option value="">Chargement...</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Chauffeur</label>
                <select class="form-control" id="id_chauffeur" required>
                    <option value="">Chargement...</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Patient</label>
                <select class="form-control" id="id_beneficiaire" required>
                    <option value="">Chargement...</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Date et heure de départ</label>
                <input type="datetime-local" class="form-control" id="date_depart" required>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Lieu de départ</label>
                <input type="text" class="form-control" id="lieu_depart" required>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Destination</label>
                <input type="text" class="form-control" id="destination" required>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Type</label>
                <select class="form-control" id="type">
                    <option value="sanitaire">Sanitaire</option>
                    <option value="touristique">Touristique</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <button class="btn btn-success" onclick="enregistrerCourse()">Planifier</button>
            <div id="message" class="mt-3"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        async function chargerVehicules() {
            const v = await API.get('/vehicules');
            const select = document.getElementById('id_vehicule');
            select.innerHTML = '<option value="">Choisir</option>';
            v.forEach(v => select.innerHTML += `<option value="${v.id_vehicule}">${v.type} (${v.immatriculation})</option>`);
        }
        async function chargerChauffeurs() {
            const p = await API.get('/personnel');
            const select = document.getElementById('id_chauffeur');
            select.innerHTML = '<option value="">Choisir</option>';
            p.forEach(p => select.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id_personnel}">${p.prenom} ${p.nom}</option>`);
        }
        async function chargerPatients() {
            const p = await API.get('/beneficiaires');
            const select = document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire');
            select.innerHTML = '<option value="">Choisir</option>';
            p.forEach(p => select.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id_beneficiaire}">${p.prenom} ${p.nom}</option>`);
        }
        chargerVehicules();
        chargerChauffeurs();
        chargerPatients();

        async function enregistrerCourse() {
            const data = {
                id_vehicule: document.getElementById('id_vehicule').value,
                id_chauffeur: document.getElementById('id_chauffeur').value,
                id_beneficiaire: document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire').value,
                date_depart: document.getElementById('date_depart').value,
                lieu_depart: document.getElementById('lieu_depart').value,
                destination: document.getElementById('destination').value,
                type: document.getElementById('type').value
            };
            if (!data.id_vehicule || !data.id_chauffeur || !data.id_beneficiaire || !data.date_depart || !data.lieu_depart || !data.destination) {
                return document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-warning">Tous les champs sont requis</div>';
            }
            try {
                const result = await API.post('/courses', data);
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-success">Course planifiée (ID ${result.id})</div>`;
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Erreur</div>';
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>

</html>

        async function chargerPatients() {
            const patients = await API.get('/beneficiaires');
            const select = document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire');
            select.innerHTML = '<option value="">Choisir un patient</option>';
            patients.forEach(p => {
                select.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id_beneficiaire}">${p.nom} ${p.prenom}</option>`;
            });
        }
        chargerPatients();

        async function enregistrerMedicament() {
            const data = {
                id_beneficiaire: document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire').value,
                medicament: document.getElementById('medicament').value,
                posologie: document.getElementById('posologie').value,
                horaire: document.getElementById('horaire').value
            };
            if (!data.id_beneficiaire || !data.medicament) return alert('Champs requis');

                const result = await API.post('/medicaments', data);
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-success">Médicament enregistré (ID ${result.id})</div>`;
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Erreur</div>';
            }
        }
    </script>

        async function enregistrerPersonnel() {
            const data = {
                nom: document.getElementById('nom').value,
                prenom: document.getElementById('prenom').value,
                poste: document.getElementById('poste').value,
                email: document.getElementById('email').value,
                telephone: document.getElementById('telephone').value,
                date_embauche: document.getElementById('date_embauche').value,
                statut: document.getElementById('statut').value
            };
            if (!data.nom || !data.prenom) {
                return document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-warning">Nom et prénom requis</div>';
            }

                const result = await API.post('/personnel', data);
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-success">Personnel ajouté (ID ${result.id})</div>`;
                document.getElementById('nom').value = '';
                document.getElementById('prenom').value = '';
                document.getElementById('poste').value = '';
                document.getElementById('email').value = '';
                document.getElementById('telephone').value = '';
                document.getElementById('date_embauche').value = '';

            }
        }
    </script>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">

<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Nouvelle prescription</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>

<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #27ae60;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-prescription"></i> Nouvelle prescription</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='dashboard-medecin.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container mt-5">
        <div class="card-custom">
            <h2 class="mb-4">Prescrire un médicament</h2>

            <!-- Sélecteur patient -->
            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Patient</label>
                <select class="form-control" id="id_beneficiaire" required>
                    <option value="">Chargement des patients...</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Médicament</label>
                <input type="text" class="form-control" id="medicament" required>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Posologie</label>
                <textarea class="form-control" id="posologie" rows="2"
                    placeholder="ex: 1 comprimé matin et soir"></textarea>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Statut</label>
                <select class="form-control" id="statut">
                    <option value="en_cours">En cours</option>
                    <option value="termine">Terminé</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <button class="btn btn-success" onclick="enregistrerPrescription()">Enregistrer</button>
            <div id="message" class="mt-3"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        // Charger les patients
        async function chargerPatients() {
            try {
                const patients = await API.get('/beneficiaires');
                const select = document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire');
                select.innerHTML = '<option value="">Choisir un patient</option>';
                patients.forEach(p => {
                    select.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id_beneficiaire}">${p.nom} ${p.prenom}</option>`;
                });
            } catch (e) {
                console.error("Erreur chargement patients", e);
            }
        }
        chargerPatients();

        // Enregistrer la prescription
        async function enregistrerPrescription() {
            const data = {
                id_beneficiaire: document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire').value,
                medicament: document.getElementById('medicament').value,
                posologie: document.getElementById('posologie').value,
                statut: document.getElementById('statut').value
            };

            if (!data.id_beneficiaire || !data.medicament) {
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-warning">Veuillez remplir tous les champs</div>';
                return;
            }

            try {
                const result = await API.post('/prescriptions', data);
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-success">Prescription enregistrée (ID ${result.id})</div>`;
                document.getElementById('medicament').value = '';
                document.getElementById('posologie').value = '';
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Erreur lors de l\'enregistrement</div>';
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>

</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">

<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Nouveau projet</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>

<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #2c3e50;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-project-diagram"></i> Nouveau projet</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='direction/projets.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container mt-5">
        <div class="card-custom">
            <h2 class="mb-4">Ajouter un projet</h2>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Nom du projet</label>
                <input type="text" class="form-control" id="nom" required>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Description</label>
                <textarea class="form-control" id="description" rows="3"></textarea>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Budget (FCFA)</label>
                <input type="number" class="form-control" id="budget" value="0" min="0">
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Avancement (%)</label>
                <input type="number" class="form-control" id="avancement" value="0" min="0" max="100">
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Statut</label>
                <select class="form-control" id="statut">
                    <option value="planifie">Planifié</option>
                    <option value="en_cours">En cours</option>
                    <option value="termine">Terminé</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <button class="btn btn-success" onclick="enregistrerProjet()">Ajouter</button>
            <div id="message" class="mt-3"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        async function enregistrerProjet() {
            const data = {
                nom: document.getElementById('nom').value,
                description: document.getElementById('description').value,
                budget: parseInt(document.getElementById('budget').value),
                avancement: parseInt(document.getElementById('avancement').value),
                statut: document.getElementById('statut').value
            };
            if (!data.nom) {
                return document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-warning">Nom requis</div>';
            }
            try {
                const result = await API.post('/projets', data);
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-success">Projet ajouté (ID ${result.id})</div>`;
                document.getElementById('nom').value = '';
                document.getElementById('description').value = '';
                document.getElementById('budget').value = 0;
                document.getElementById('avancement').value = 0;
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Erreur</div>';
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>

</html>

    <script>
        async function enregistrerRapport() {
            const data = {
                nom: document.getElementById('nom').value,
                periode: document.getElementById('periode').value,
                taille: document.getElementById('taille').value,
                url: document.getElementById('url').value
            };
            if (!data.nom || !data.periode || !data.taille || !data.url) {
                return document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-warning">Tous les champs sont requis</div>';
            }
            try {
                const result = await API.post('/rapports', data);
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-success">Rapport ajouté (ID ${result.id})</div>`;
                document.getElementById('nom').value = '';
                document.getElementById('periode').value = '';
                document.getElementById('taille').value = '';
                document.getElementById('url').value = '';
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Erreur</div>';
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>

</html>

=== FICHIER: ajout-rendezvous.html ===
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Nouveau rendez-vous</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>
<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #3498db;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-calendar-plus"></i> Nouveau rendez-vous</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='dashboard-patient.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container mt-5">
        <div class="card-custom">
            <h2 class="mb-4">Prendre un rendez-vous</h2>
            
            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Médecin</label>
                <select class="form-control" id="id_medecin" required>
                    <option value="">Chargement...</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Date et heure</label>
                <input type="datetime-local" class="form-control" id="date_rdv" required>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Motif</label>
                <textarea class="form-control" id="motif" rows="3"></textarea>
            </div>

            <button class="btn btn-success" onclick="enregistrerRdv()">Prendre rendez-vous</button>
            <div id="message" class="mt-3"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        async function chargerMedecins() {
            try {
                const medecins = await API.get('/personnel/medecins');
                const select = document.getElementById('id_medecin');
                select.innerHTML = '<option value="">Choisir un médecin</option>';
                medecins.forEach(m => {
                    select.innerHTML += `<option value="${m.id_personnel}">Dr. ${m.prenom} ${m.nom}</option>`;
                });
            } catch (e) {
                console.error("Erreur chargement médecins", e);
            }
        }
        chargerMedecins();

        async function enregistrerRdv() {
    const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
    console.log('🔍 token:', token);
    
    if (!token) {
        window.location.href = 'index.html';
        return;
    }
    
    const payload = JSON.parse(atob(token.split('.')[1]));
    const id_beneficiaire = payload.id;

    // ✅ Définir data AVANT de l'utiliser
    const data = {
        id_beneficiaire: id_beneficiaire,
        id_medecin: document.getElementById('id_medecin').value,
        date_rdv: document.getElementById('date_rdv').value,
        motif: document.getElementById('motif').value
    };

    console.log('📤 données envoyées:', data);

    if (!data.id_medecin || !data.date_rdv) {
        document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-warning">Veuillez remplir tous les champs</div>';
        return;
    }

    try {
        const result = await API.post('/rendez-vous', data);
        document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-success">Rendez-vous enregistré (ID ${result.id})</div>`;
        document.getElementById('date_rdv').value = '';
        document.getElementById('motif').value = '';
    } catch (e) {
        document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Erreur</div>';
    }
}
    </script>
</body>
</html>

=== FICHIER: ajout-soin.html ===
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">

<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Nouveau soin</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>

<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #1abc9c;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-hand-holding-medical"></i> Nouveau soin</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm"
                onclick="window.location.href='dashboard-infirmier.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container mt-5">
        <div class="card-custom">
            <h2 class="mb-4">Programmer un soin</h2>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Patient</label>
                <select class="form-control" id="id_beneficiaire" required>
                    <option value="">Chargement...</option>
                </select>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3">
                <label>Type de soin</label>
                <input type="text" class="form-control" id="type_soin" placeholder="ex: Pansement, Injection..."
                    required>
            </div>

            <div class="mb-3 form-check">
                <input type="checkbox" class="form-check-input" id="urgent">
                <label class="form-check-label">Urgent</label>
            </div>

            <button class="btn btn-success" onclick="enregistrerSoin()">Programmer</button>
            <div id="message" class="mt-3"></div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        async function chargerPatients() {
            const patients = await API.get('/beneficiaires');
            const select = document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire');
            select.innerHTML = '<option value="">Choisir un patient</option>';
            patients.forEach(p => {
                select.innerHTML += `<option value="${p.id_beneficiaire}">${p.nom} ${p.prenom}</option>`;
            });
        }
        chargerPatients();

        async function enregistrerSoin() {
            const data = {
                id_beneficiaire: document.getElementById('id_beneficiaire').value,
                type_soin: document.getElementById('type_soin').value,
                urgent: document.getElementById('urgent').checked ? 1 : 0
            };
            if (!data.id_beneficiaire || !data.type_soin) {
                return document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-warning">Tous les champs requis</div>';
            }
            try {
                const result = await API.post('/soins', data);
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = `<div class="alert alert-success">Soin programmé (ID ${result.id})</div>`;
                document.getElementById('type_soin').value = '';
                document.getElementById('urgent').checked = false;
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('message').innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Erreur</div>';
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>

</html>

            <div id="step3" class="step-content">
                <div class="success-animation">
                    <div class="checkmark-circle"><i class="fas fa-check"></i></div>
                    <h2 class="fw-bold text-success mb-3">Connexion réussie !</h2>
                    <p class="text-muted mb-4">Redirection vers votre espace patient</p>
                    <div class="loading-dots"><div></div><div></div><div></div></div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        console.log('✅ Script chargé');
        let countdownInterval;
        let timeLeft = 120;
        let currentPhone = '';

        function showError(message) {
            const errorDiv = document.getElementById('errorMessage');
            document.getElementById('errorText').textContent = message;
            errorDiv.classList.remove('d-none');
            console.log('⏱️ Lancement du setTimeou unique 01');
            setTimeout(() => errorDiv.classList.add('d-none'), 3000);
        }

        function updateSteps(step) {
            ['step1-indicator', 'step2-indicator', 'step3-indicator'].forEach(id => {
                document.getElementById(id).classList.remove('active', 'completed');
            });
            if (step === 1) {
                document.getElementById('step1-indicator').classList.add('active');
            } else if (step === 2) {
                document.getElementById('step1-indicator').classList.add('completed');
                document.getElementById('step2-indicator').classList.add('active');
            } else if (step === 3) {
                document.getElementById('step1-indicator').classList.add('completed');
                document.getElementById('step2-indicator').classList.add('completed');
                document.getElementById('step3-indicator').classList.add('active');
            }
        }

        function envoyerCode() {
            const phone = document.getElementById('phone').value;
            const terms = document.getElementById('terms').checked;

            if (!phone) {
                showError('Veuillez entrer votre numéro');
                document.getElementById('phone').classList.add('error');
                console.log('⏱️ Lancement du setTimeou unique 02');
                setTimeout(() => document.getElementById('phone').classList.remove('error'), 500);
                return;
            }
            if (!terms) {
                showError('Veuillez accepter les conditions');
                return;
            }

            fetch('/api/whatsapp/request-code', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ telephone: phone })
            })
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => {
                if (data.success) {
                    currentPhone = phone;
                    document.getElementById('step1').classList.remove('active');
                    document.getElementById('step2').classList.add('active');
                    updateSteps(2);
                    document.getElementById('phoneDisplay').textContent = phone;
                    startCountdown();
                    if (data.code_dev) {
                        console.log('📱 Code de test (à des fins de développement) :', data.code_dev);
                    }
                } else {
                    showError(data.error || 'Erreur serveur');
                }
            })
            .catch(() => showError('Erreur de connexion au serveur'));
        }

        function verifierCode() {
            

            const inputs = document.querySelectorAll('.code-box');
            let code = '';
            inputs.forEach(input => code += input.value);

            if (code.length < 6) {
                showError('Code incomplet');
                return;
            }

            console.log('📤 Envoi du code au serveur...', code);

            fetch('/api/whatsapp/verify-code', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ telephone: currentPhone, code: code })
            })
            .then(res => {
                console.log('📥 Statut HTTP :', res.status);
                return res.json();
            })
            .then(data => {
                console.log('📥 Réponse du serveur :', JSON.stringify(data));
                if (data.success) {
                    document.getElementById('step2').classList.remove('active');
                    document.getElementById('step3').classList.add('active');
                    updateSteps(3);

                    if (data.token) {
                        localStorage.setItem('token', data.token);
                    }
                    if (data.user) {
                        localStorage.setItem('user', JSON.stringify(data.user));
                    }

                    setTimeout(() => {
                        if (data.tempToken) {
                            window.location.href = `inscription-patient.html?tel=${encodeURIComponent(currentPhone)}&token=${data.tempToken}`;
                        } else {
                            window.location.href = data.redirect || 'dashboard-patient.html';
                        }
                    }, 2000);
                } else {
                    showError(data.error || 'Code incorrect');
                    inputs.forEach(input => { input.value = ''; input.classList.remove('filled'); });
                    inputs[0].focus();
                }
            })
            .catch(err => {
                console.error('❌ Erreur fetch :', err);
                showError('Erreur de connexion au serveur');
            });
        }

        function moveToNext(current, nextIndex) {
            if (current.value.length === 1 && nextIndex < 6) {
                const next = document.querySelectorAll('.code-box')[nextIndex];
                if (next) next.focus();
            }
        }

        function checkFilled(input) {
            if (input.value.length === 1) {
                input.classList.add('filled');
            } else {
                input.classList.remove('filled');
            }
        }

        function startCountdown() {
            timeLeft = 120;
            updateCountdown();
            countdownInterval = setInterval(() => {
                timeLeft--;
                updateCountdown();
                if (timeLeft <= 0) {
                    clearInterval(countdownInterval);
                    document.getElementById('countdown').innerHTML = '00:00';
                    document.getElementById('countdown').classList.add('warning');
                    showError('Code expiré. Veuillez renvoyer un code.');
                }
            }, 1000);
        }

        function updateCountdown() {
            const minutes = Math.floor(timeLeft / 60);
            const seconds = timeLeft % 60;
            const countdown = document.getElementById('countdown');
            countdown.textContent = `${minutes.toString().padStart(2, '0')}:${seconds.toString().padStart(2, '0')}`;
            if (timeLeft <= 30) {
                countdown.classList.add('warning');
            }
        }

        function renvoyerCode() {
            clearInterval(countdownInterval);
            fetch('/api/whatsapp/request-code', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ telephone: currentPhone })
            })
            .then(res => res.json())
            .then(data => {
                if (data.success) {
                    startCountdown();
                } else {
                    showError(data.error || 'Erreur');
                }
            })
            .catch(() => showError('Erreur de connexion'));
        }

        function retourEtape1() {
            clearInterval(countdownInterval);
            document.getElementById('step2').classList.remove('active');
            document.getElementById('step1').classList.add('active');
            updateSteps(1);
        }
    </script>
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        (async function () {

            <div class="col-md-3"><div class="stat-card" style="border-left-color:#27ae60;"><div class="stat-value">${stats.personnel_actif || 28}</div><div class="stat-label">Personnel</div></div></div>
        `;

        // Affichage des factures

                    <strong>Facture #${f.id_facture}</strong> – ${f.nom} ${f.prenom}<br>

                    <span class="badge-custom badge-${f.statut === 'payee' ? 'success' : 'warning'}">${f.statut}</span>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        } else {
            container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted text-center">Aucune facture trouvée</p>';
        }

    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Erreur chargement admin :', e);
    }
})();
    </script>

                // Graphiques
                if (stats.graphiques && Array.isArray(stats.graphiques.caMensuel)) {
    // Graphique CA
    const ctx = document.getElementById('caChart').getContext('2d');
    new Chart(ctx, {
        type: 'line',
        data: {
            labels: ['Jan', 'Fév', 'Mar', 'Avr', 'Mai', 'Juin'],
            datasets: [{
                label: 'CA (DA)',
                data: stats.graphiques.caMensuel,
                borderColor: '#3498db',
                backgroundColor: 'rgba(52,152,219,0.1)',
                borderWidth: 2,
                tension: 0.3,
                fill: true
            }]
        },
        options: {
            responsive: true,
            maintainAspectRatio: false,
            animation: {
                duration: 1000 // limite l'animation
            },
            scales: {
                y: {
                    beginAtZero: true,
                    ticks: {
                        callback: function(value) {
                            return value / 1000000 + 'M';
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    });

    // Graphique dépenses
    const ctx2 = document.getElementById('depensesChart').getContext('2d');
    new Chart(ctx2, {
        type: 'doughnut',
        data: {
            labels: ['Salaires', 'Médicaments', 'Équipement', 'Maintenance', 'Autres'],
            datasets: [{
                data: Object.values(stats.graphiques.repartitionDepenses),
                backgroundColor: ['#3498db', '#e74c3c', '#f39c12', '#9b59b6', '#95a5a6']
            }]
        },
        options: {
            responsive: true,
            maintainAspectRatio: false,
            animation: {
                duration: 1000
            }
        }
    });
}
            } catch (e) {

            }
        })();

                <i class="fas fa-users"></i><span>Patients</span>

                <i class="fas fa-calendar-check"></i><span>Rendez-vous</span>

                <div class="loading-spinner"></div>

    <script>
        (async function () {
    try {
        // 1. Récupérer les vraies statistiques
        const stats = await API.getStats();

        // 2. Récupérer les vraies consultations (avec jointure)
        const consultations = await API.getConsultations();

        // 3. Récupérer les vrais rendez-vous (avec jointure)
        const rdvs = await API.getRendezVous();

        // Affichage des stats
        const statsRow = document.getElementById('statsRow');
        statsRow.innerHTML = `
            <div class="col-md-3">
                <div class="stat-card"><div class="stat-value">${stats.consultations_jour || 0}</div><div class="stat-label">Consultations</div></div>
            </div>
            <div class="col-md-3">
                <div class="stat-card" style="border-left-color: #27ae60;"><div class="stat-value">${stats.patients_total || 0}</div><div class="stat-label">Patients</div></div>
            </div>
            <div class="col-md-3">
                <div class="stat-card" style="border-left-color: #f39c12;"><div class="stat-value">${stats.rdv_jour || 0}</div><div class="stat-label">Rendez-vous</div></div>
            </div>
            <div class="col-md-3">
                <div class="stat-card" style="border-left-color: #e74c3c;"><div class="stat-value">${stats.rdv_attente || 0}</div><div class="stat-label">En attente</div></div>
            </div>
        `;

        // Affichage des consultations
        const consContainer = document.getElementById('consultationsContainer');
        if (consultations.length) {
            consContainer.innerHTML = consultations.map(c => `
                <div class="consultation-card">
                    <div><strong>${new Date(c.date_heure).toLocaleString()}</strong></div>
                    <div>Patient : ${c.patientNom || '?'} ${c.patientPrenom || '?'}</div>
                    <div class="text-muted">Motif : ${c.motif || 'Non précisé'}</div>
                    <span class="badge-custom badge-${c.statut === 'realisee' ? 'success' : 'warning'}">${c.statut}</span>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        } else {
            consContainer.innerHTML = '<p class="text-center text-muted">Aucune consultation récente</p>';
        }

        // Affichage des rendez-vous
        const rdvContainer = document.getElementById('rdvContainer');
        if (rdvs.length) {
            rdvContainer.innerHTML = rdvs.map(r => `
                <div class="consultation-card">
                    <div><strong>${new Date(r.date_rdv).toLocaleString()}</strong> - ${r.nom} ${r.prenom}</div>
                    <div class="text-muted">Motif : ${r.motif || 'Consultation'}</div>
                    <span class="badge-custom badge-${r.statut === 'confirmé' ? 'success' : 'warning'}">${r.statut}</span>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        } else {
            rdvContainer.innerHTML = '<p class="text-center text-muted">Aucun rendez-vous prévu</p>';
        }

    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Erreur chargement dashboard médecin :', e);
    }
})();
    </script>
</body>

</html>
