<script>
    let currentPatientId = null;
    
    function updateDate() {
        const options = { weekday: 'long', year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' };
        document.getElementById('current-date').textContent = new Date().toLocaleDateString('fr-FR', options);
    }
    
    function showPatientSection(section) {
        document.querySelectorAll('.patient-section').forEach(s => s.classList.remove('active'));
        document.getElementById('patient-' + section).classList.add('active');
        
        document.querySelectorAll('.patient-menu a').forEach(link => link.classList.remove('active'));
        const links = document.querySelectorAll('.patient-menu a');
        for (let link of links) {
            if (link.getAttribute('onclick')?.includes(section)) {
                link.classList.add('active');
                break;
            }
        }
    }
    
    async function loadPatientData() {
    const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
    if (!token) {
        window.location.href = 'index.html';
        return;
    }

    try {
        const payload = JSON.parse(atob(token.split('.')[1]));
        currentPatientId = payload.id;

        // Récupérer les infos du patient depuis l'API
        const response = await fetch(`https://clinique-hoteliere-et-actions.onrender.com/api/beneficiaires/${currentPatientId}`);
        const patient = await response.json();

        // Mettre à jour l'interface
        document.getElementById('user-name').textContent = `${patient.prenom || ''} ${patient.nom || ''}`;
        document.getElementById('user-info').textContent = `N° ${currentPatientId}`;
        document.getElementById('sidebar-name').textContent = `${patient.prenom || ''} ${patient.nom || ''}`;
        document.getElementById('sidebar-email').textContent = patient.email || 'Non renseigné';
        document.getElementById('sidebar-phone').textContent = patient.telephone || 'Non renseigné';
        document.getElementById('sidebar-id').textContent = currentPatientId;

        const initiales = (patient.prenom?.[0] || 'P') + (patient.nom?.[0] || '');
        document.getElementById('user-initials').textContent = initiales;
        document.getElementById('sidebar-avatar').textContent = initiales;

        // Récupérer les vrais rendez-vous
        await chargerRendezVous(currentPatientId);

        // Récupérer les vraies prescriptions
        await chargerPrescriptions(currentPatientId);

        // Récupérer les vraies factures
        await chargerFactures(currentPatientId);

    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Erreur chargement patient:', e);
        window.location.href = 'index.html';
    }
}
async function chargerRendezVous(patientId) {
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`https://clinique-hoteliere-et-actions.onrender.com/api/rendez-vous/patient/${patientId}`);
        const rdvs = await response.json();
        const container = document.getElementById('prochains-rdv-container');
        
        if (rdvs && rdvs.length > 0) {
            container.innerHTML = rdvs.map(r => `
                <div class="col-md-6">
                    <div class="consultation-card">
                        <div><strong>${new Date(r.date_rdv).toLocaleDateString()} ${new Date(r.date_rdv).toLocaleTimeString()}</strong> - ${r.medecin_nom || 'Médecin'}</div>
                        <div>${r.motif || 'Consultation'}</div>
                        <span class="badge-custom badge-success">${r.statut}</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `).join('');
            document.getElementById('prochains-rdv').textContent = rdvs.length;
        } else {
            container.innerHTML = '<div class="col-12 text-center text-muted py-4">Aucun rendez-vous prévu</div>';
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Erreur chargement rendez-vous:', e);
    }
}

async function chargerPrescriptions(patientId) {
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`https://clinique-hoteliere-et-actions.onrender.com/api/prescriptions/patient/${patientId}`);
        const prescriptions = await response.json();
        const container = document.getElementById('dernieres-prescriptions-container');
        
        if (prescriptions && prescriptions.length > 0) {
            container.innerHTML = prescriptions.map(p => `
                <div class="prescription-card">
                    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between">
                        <div>
                            <div class="prescription-title">${p.medicament}</div>
                            <div class="prescription-date">Prescrit le ${new Date(p.date_prescription).toLocaleDateString()}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="prescription-doctor">${p.medecin_nom || 'Médecin'}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mt-2 small">
                        <span class="badge bg-warning">${p.statut}</span>
                        <span class="ms-2">${p.posologie}</span>
                    </div>
                </div>
            `).join('');
            document.getElementById('prescriptions-actives').textContent = prescriptions.length;
        } else {
            container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-center text-muted py-3">Aucune prescription</p>';
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Erreur chargement prescriptions:', e);
    }
}

async function chargerFactures(patientId) {
    try {
        const response = await fetch(`https://clinique-hoteliere-et-actions.onrender.com/api/factures/patient/${patientId}`);
        const factures = await response.json();
        const container = document.getElementById('factures-table-body');
        
        if (factures && factures.length > 0) {
            container.innerHTML = factures.map(f => `
                <div class="consultation-card mb-2">
                    <strong>Facture ${f.numero || f.id_facture}</strong><br>
                    Date : ${new Date(f.date_emission).toLocaleDateString()}<br>
                    Montant : ${f.montant_ttc} FCFA<br>
                    <span class="badge-custom badge-${f.statut === 'payee' ? 'success' : 'warning'}">${f.statut}</span>
                </div>
            `).join('');
            document.getElementById('factures-attente').textContent = factures.filter(f => f.statut !== 'payee').length;
        } else {
            container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted text-center py-3">Aucune facture</p>';
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Erreur chargement factures:', e);
    }
}
    
    function prendreRendezVous() {    window.location.href = 'ajout-rendezvous.html';}
   function consulterDossier() {    window.location.href = 'dossier-patient.html';}
    function contacterMedecin() { alert('Formulaire de contact médecin'); }
    function payerFacture() { showPatientSection('factures'); }
    function voirTousRdv() {    window.location.href = 'mes-rdv.html';}
   function voirMessages() {    window.location.href = 'messages-patient.html';}
   function voirDocuments() {    window.location.href = 'documents-patient.html';}
    function prescriptions() {    window.location.href = 'prescriptions-patient.html';}
    function deconnexion() { localStorage.removeItem('token'); localStorage.removeItem('user'); window.location.href = 'index.html'; }
   function voirFactures() {
    console.log('voirFactures() appelée');
    window.location.href = 'factures-patient.html';
}

    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        updateDate();
        loadPatientData();
        setInterval(updateDate, 60000);
    });
</script>

<!-- Bootstrap JS -->
<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>

</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">

        function chargerDocuments() {
            console.log('chargerDocuments() exécuté');
            const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
            if (!token) {
                return;
            }

            // Simuler des documents
            const documents = [
                { nom: "Compte-rendu consultation 15-03-26.pdf", date: "15/03/2026", taille: "245 Ko" },
                { nom: "Radio thorax 28-02-26.jpg", date: "28/02/2026", taille: "1.2 Mo" },
                { nom: "Prescription Amoxicilline 15-03-26.pdf", date: "15/03/2026", taille: "124 Ko" }
            ];

            const container = document.getElementById('documentsContainer');
            if (documents.length) {
                container.innerHTML = documents.map(d => `
                    <div class="consultation-card mb-2">
                        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
                            <div>
                                <strong>${d.nom}</strong><br>
                                <small class="text-muted">${d.date} • ${d.taille}</small>
                            </div>
                            <button class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" onclick="alert('Téléchargement de ${d.nom}')">
                                <i class="fas fa-download"></i>
                            </button>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `).join('');
            } else {
                container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucun document.</p>';
            }
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', chargerDocuments);
    </script>

    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #3498db;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-folder-open"></i> Mon dossier médical</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='dashboard-patient.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container-fluid px-4 py-4">
        <h2>Informations médicales</h2>
        <div id="dossierContainer" class="loading-container mt-4">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Chargement de votre dossier...</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        async function chargerDossier() {
            const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
            if (!token) {
                window.location.href = 'index.html';
                return;
            }

            const payload = JSON.parse(atob(token.split('.')[1]));
            const id_beneficiaire = payload.id;

            try {
                // Simuler des données en attendant la vraie route API
                const dossier = {
                    groupe_sanguin: 'A+',
                    allergies: 'Pénicilline',
                    antecedents: 'Hypertension (2020), Appendicite (2018)',
                    traitements: 'Amlodipine 5mg',
                    medecin_traitant: 'Dr. Mamadou Diallo'
                };

                const container = document.getElementById('dossierContainer');
                container.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="card-custom">
                        <p><strong>Groupe sanguin :</strong> ${dossier.groupe_sanguin}</p>
                        <p><strong>Allergies :</strong> ${dossier.allergies}</p>
                        <p><strong>Antécédents :</strong> ${dossier.antecedents}</p>
                        <p><strong>Traitements en cours :</strong> ${dossier.traitements}</p>
                        <p><strong>Médecin traitant :</strong> ${dossier.medecin_traitant}</p>
                    </div>
                `;
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('dossierContainer').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger">Erreur chargement.</p>';
            }
        }

        chargerDossier();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        async function chargerFactures() {
            console.log('chargerFactures() exécuté');
            const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
            if (!token) {
               // window.location.href = 'index.html';
                return;
            }

            const payload = JSON.parse(atob(token.split('.')[1]));
            const id_beneficiaire = payload.id;

            try {
                // Simuler des données en attendant la vraie route API
                const factures = [
                    { numero: "FAC-001", date: "01/03/2026", montant: "49 500", statut: "payee" },
                    { numero: "FAC-002", date: "05/03/2026", montant: "27 500", statut: "en_attente" },
                    { numero: "FAC-003", date: "08/03/2026", montant: "137 500", statut: "impayee" }
                ];

                const container = document.getElementById('facturesContainer');
                if (factures.length) {
                    container.innerHTML = factures.map(f => `
                        <div class="consultation-card mb-2">
                            <strong>Facture ${f.numero}</strong><br>
                            Date : ${f.date}<br>
                            Montant : ${f.montant} DA<br>
                            <span class="badge-custom badge-${f.statut === 'payee' ? 'success' : f.statut === 'en_attente' ? 'warning' : 'danger'}">${f.statut}</span>
                        </div>
                    `).join('');
                } else {
                    container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucune facture trouvée.</p>';
                }
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('facturesContainer').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger">Erreur chargement.</p>';
            }
        }

       // chargerFactures();
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', chargerFactures);
    </script>
</body>

<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #e67e22;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-hotel"></i> Service hôtellerie</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='index.html'">Accueil</button>
        </div>
    </nav>
    <div class="container-fluid px-4 mt-3">
        <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="window.location.href='ajout-chambre.html'">
            <i class="fas fa-plus"></i> Nouvelle chambre
        </button>
        <button class="btn btn-primary ms-2" onclick="window.location.href='ajout-commande.html'">
            <i class="fas fa-plus"></i> Nouvelle commande
        </button>
    </div>

    <div class="container-fluid px-4 py-4">
        <h2>Occupation des chambres</h2>
        <div id="chambresList" class="loading-container mt-4">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Chargement des chambres...</p>
        </div>

        <h2 class="mt-5">Commandes repas</h2>
        <div id="commandesList" class="loading-container mt-4">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Chargement des commandes...</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        (async function () {
            try {
                // Chambres
                const chambres = await API.get('/chambres');
                const chambresContainer = document.getElementById('chambresList');
                if (chambres.length) {
                    chambresContainer.innerHTML = chambres.map(c => `
                        <div class="consultation-card mb-2" style="border-left-color: #e67e22;">
                            <strong>Chambre ${c.numero}</strong> (${c.type})<br>
                            Capacité : ${c.capacite} personne(s)<br>
                            Statut : <span class="badge-custom badge-${c.statut === 'libre' ? 'success' : c.statut === 'occupee' ? 'info' : 'warning'}">${c.statut}</span>
                        </div>
                    `).join('');
                } else {
                    chambresContainer.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucune chambre trouvée.</p>';
                }

                // Commandes repas
                const commandes = await API.get('/commandes');
                const commandesContainer = document.getElementById('commandesList');
                if (commandes.length) {
                    commandesContainer.innerHTML = commandes.map(cmd => `
                        <div class="consultation-card mb-2" style="border-left-color: #e67e22;">
                            <strong>Patient : ${cmd.nom} ${cmd.prenom}</strong><br>
                            Service : ${cmd.type_service}<br>
                            Statut : <span class="badge-custom badge-${cmd.statut === 'livre' ? 'success' : cmd.statut === 'pret' ? 'info' : 'warning'}">${cmd.statut}</span>
                        </div>
                    `).join('');
                } else {
                    commandesContainer.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucune commande trouvée.</p>';
                }

            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('chambresList').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger">Erreur chargement.</p>';
            }
        })();
    </script>
</body>

</html>

    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
    <script src="https://unpkg.com/aos@2.3.1/dist/aos.js"></script>

    <script>
        AOS.init({ duration: 1000 });

        window.addEventListener('scroll', function () {
            const navbar = document.querySelector('.navbar');
            if (window.scrollY > 50) {
                navbar.classList.add('scrolled');
            } else {
                navbar.classList.remove('scrolled');
            }
        });

        function selectProfil(profil, element) {
            document.querySelectorAll('.profil-option').forEach(opt => opt.classList.remove('selected'));
            element.classList.add('selected');
            document.getElementById('profil-select').value = profil;
        }

        function login() {
            const profil = document.getElementById('profil-select').value;
            const username = document.getElementById('username').value;
            const password = document.getElementById('password').value;

            const redirections = {
                'medecin': 'dashboard-medecin.html',
                'infirmier': 'dashboard-infirmier.html',
                'direction': 'dashboard-direction.html',
                'administratif': 'dashboard-admin.html',
                'hotellerie': 'hotellerie.html',
                'logistique': 'stocks.html',
                'qualite': 'qualite.html',
                'voyages': 'voyages.html'
            };

            window.location.href = redirections[profil];
        }
    </script>
</body>

<html lang="fr">

<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Inscription Patient - Hôpital Saint-Jean</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <!-- Notre CSS personnalisé -->
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/chart.js"></script>
    <script src="js/api.js"></script>

</head>

<body>
    <div class="inscription-container">
        <div class="header">
            <i class="fab fa-whatsapp"></i>
            <h2>Finalisez votre inscription</h2>
        </div>

        <div class="body">
            <div id="successAlert" class="alert alert-success"></div>
            <div id="errorAlert" class="alert alert-danger"></div>

            <div class="phone-display">
                <i class="fas fa-phone-alt me-2"></i>
                Numéro vérifié :
                <span id="displayPhone">Chargement...</span>
            </div>

            <form id="inscriptionForm">
                <div class="row">
                    <div class="col-md-6">
                        <input type="text" class="form-control" id="nom" placeholder="Nom" required>
                    </div>
                    <div class="col-md-6">
                        <input type="text" class="form-control" id="prenom" placeholder="Prénom" required>
                    </div>
                </div>

                <input type="date" class="form-control" id="dateNaissance" required>
                <input type="email" class="form-control" id="email" placeholder="Email" required>
                <input type="text" class="form-control" id="adresse" placeholder="Adresse" required>

                <select class="form-control" id="groupeSanguin">
                    <option value="">Groupe sanguin</option>
                    <option>A+</option>
                    <option>A-</option>
                    <option>B+</option>
                    <option>B-</option>
                    <option>AB+</option>
                    <option>AB-</option>
                    <option>O+</option>
                    <option>O-</option>
                </select>

                <input type="text" class="form-control" id="allergies" placeholder="Allergies (optionnel)">

                <button type="submit" class="btn-inscription" id="submitBtn">
                    <i class="fas fa-check-circle me-2"></i>
                    Créer mon compte
                </button>

                <div id="spinner" class="spinner"></div>
            </form>

            <div class="text-center mt-3">
                <a href="connexion-whatsapp.html" class="text-decoration-none">
                    <i class="fas fa-arrow-left me-2"></i>
                    Retour
                </a>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        
    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const telephone = urlParams.get('tel');
    const tempToken = urlParams.get('token');

    document.getElementById('displayPhone').textContent = telephone || 'Numéro inconnu';

    function showSuccess(message) {
        const alert = document.getElementById('successAlert');
        alert.textContent = message;
        alert.style.display = 'block';
        setTimeout(() => alert.style.display = 'none', 3000);
    }

    function showError(message) {
        const alert = document.getElementById('errorAlert');
        alert.textContent = message;
        alert.style.display = 'block';
        setTimeout(() => alert.style.display = 'none', 3000);
    }

    function showLoading(show) {
        document.getElementById('spinner').style.display = show ? 'block' : 'none';
        document.getElementById('submitBtn').disabled = show;
    }

    document.getElementById('inscriptionForm').addEventListener('submit', async (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();

        const formData = {
            telephone: telephone,
            whatsapp: telephone,
            nom: document.getElementById('nom').value,
            prenom: document.getElementById('prenom').value,
            date_naissance: document.getElementById('dateNaissance').value,
            email: document.getElementById('email').value,
            adresse: document.getElementById('adresse').value,
            groupe_sanguin: document.getElementById('groupeSanguin').value,
            allergies: document.getElementById('allergies').value || 'Aucune',
            type: 'patient'
        };

        showLoading(true);

        try {
            const response = await fetch('https://clinique-hoteliere-et-actions.onrender.com/api/beneficiaires', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'Authorization': `Bearer ${tempToken}`
                },
                body: JSON.stringify(formData)
            });

            const data = await response.json();

            if (response.ok) {
                localStorage.setItem('token', data.token);
                console.log('Token stocké :', data.token);
                showSuccess('✅ Inscription réussie !');
                setTimeout(() => {
                    window.location.href = 'dashboard-patient.html';
                }, 2000);
            } else {
                showError(data.error || 'Erreur lors de l\'inscription');
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Erreur réseau :', error);
            showError('Erreur de connexion');
        } finally {
            showLoading(false);
        }
    });
    </script>
</body>

</html>

=== FICHIER: mes-rdv.html ===
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Mes rendez-vous - Hôpital Saint-Jean</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>
<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #3498db;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-calendar-check"></i> Mes rendez-vous</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='dashboard-patient.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container-fluid px-4 py-4">
        <h2>Vos rendez-vous</h2>
        <div id="rdvList" class="loading-container mt-4">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Chargement de vos rendez-vous...</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        async function chargerRdv() {
            const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
            if (!token) {
                window.location.href = 'index.html';
                return;
            }

            const payload = JSON.parse(atob(token.split('.')[1]));
            const id_beneficiaire = payload.id;

            try {
                const rdvs = await API.get('/rendez-vous');
                const container = document.getElementById('rdvList');

                // Filtrer les rendez-vous du patient connecté
                const mesRdvs = rdvs.filter(r => r.id_beneficiaire === id_beneficiaire);

                if (mesRdvs.length) {
                    container.innerHTML = mesRdvs.map(r => `
                        <div class="consultation-card mb-2">
                            <strong>${new Date(r.date_rdv).toLocaleDateString('fr-FR')} à ${new Date(r.date_rdv).toLocaleTimeString('fr-FR', {hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit'})}</strong><br>
                            Motif : ${r.motif || 'Non précisé'}<br>
                            Statut : <span class="badge-custom badge-${r.statut === 'confirmé' ? 'success' : 'warning'}">${r.statut}</span>
                        </div>
                    `).join('');
                } else {
                    container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucun rendez-vous trouvé.</p>';
                }
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('rdvList').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger">Erreur chargement.</p>';
            }
        }

        chargerRdv();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Mes messages - Hôpital Saint-Jean</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>
<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #3498db;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-envelope"></i> Mes messages</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='dashboard-patient.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container-fluid px-4 py-4">
        <h2>Votre messagerie</h2>
        <div id="messagesContainer" class="loading-container mt-4">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Chargement de vos messages...</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        function chargerMessages() {
            console.log('chargerMessages() exécuté');
            const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
            if (!token) {
                return;
            }

            // Simuler des messages
            const messages = [
                { expediteur: "Dr. Diallo", date: "19/03/2026", contenu: "Vos résultats d'analyse sont disponibles.", lu: false },
                { expediteur: "Secrétariat", date: "18/03/2026", contenu: "Rappel : rendez-vous le 25/03 à 09h30.", lu: true },
                { expediteur: "Service facturation", date: "17/03/2026", contenu: "Votre facture du 10/03 est disponible.", lu: true }
            ];

            const container = document.getElementById('messagesContainer');
            if (messages.length) {
                container.innerHTML = messages.map(m => `
                    <div class="consultation-card mb-2 ${!m.lu ? 'unread' : ''}">
                        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between">
                            <strong>${m.expediteur}</strong>
                            <small class="text-muted">${m.date}</small>
                        </div>
                        <p class="mb-1">${m.contenu}</p>
                        ${!m.lu ? '<span class="badge-custom badge-info">Nouveau</span>' : ''}
                    </div>
                `).join('');
            } else {
                container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucun message.</p>';
            }
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', chargerMessages);
    </script>
</body>
</html>

=== FICHIER: parametres.html ===
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">

<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Paramètres - Hôpital Saint-Jean</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>

<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #95a5a6;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-cog"></i> Paramètres</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='index.html'">Accueil</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container-fluid px-4 py-4">
        <h2>Configuration</h2>
        <div id="parametresContainer" class="row"></div>
    </div>

    <script>
        (async function () {
            try {
                const params = await API.get('/parametres');
                const container = document.getElementById('parametresContainer');
                if (params.length) {
                    // Grouper par catégories (simulées)
                    const etablissement = params.filter(p => ['nom_etablissement', 'adresse', 'telephone'].includes(p.cle));
                    const preferences = params.filter(p => ['langue', 'fuseau_horaire'].includes(p.cle));

                    container.innerHTML = `
                        <div class="col-md-6">
                            <div class="card-custom">
                                <h5>Établissement</h5>
                                ${etablissement.map(p => `<p><strong>${p.description} :</strong> ${p.valeur}</p>`).join('')}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="col-md-6">
                            <div class="card-custom">
                                <h5>Préférences</h5>
                                ${preferences.map(p => `<p><strong>${p.description} :</strong> ${p.valeur}</p>`).join('')}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    `;
                } else {
                    container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucun paramètre trouvé.</p>';
                }

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Mes prescriptions - Hôpital Saint-Jean</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="css/style.css">
    <script src="/js/api.js"></script>
</head>
<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #27ae60;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-prescription"></i> Mes prescriptions</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm" onclick="window.location.href='dashboard-patient.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container-fluid px-4 py-4">
        <h2>Vos prescriptions</h2>
        <div id="prescriptionsContainer" class="loading-container mt-4">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Chargement de vos prescriptions...</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        async function chargerPrescriptions() {
            const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
            if (!token) {
                window.location.href = 'index.html';
                return;
            }

            const payload = JSON.parse(atob(token.split('.')[1]));
            const id_beneficiaire = payload.id;

            try {
                // Simuler des données en attendant la vraie route API
                const prescriptions = [
                    { medicament: "Amoxicilline 500mg", posologie: "1 comprimé 3x/jour", date: "15/03/2026", statut: "en_cours" },
                    { medicament: "Paracétamol 1000mg", posologie: "1 comprimé si douleur", date: "10/03/2026", statut: "termine" }
                ];

                const container = document.getElementById('prescriptionsContainer');
                if (prescriptions.length) {
                    container.innerHTML = prescriptions.map(p => `
                        <div class="consultation-card mb-2">
                            <strong>${p.medicament}</strong><br>
                            ${p.posologie}<br>
                            Prescrit le : ${p.date}<br>
                            <span class="badge-custom badge-${p.statut === 'en_cours' ? 'warning' : 'success'}">${p.statut}</span>
                        </div>
                    `).join('');
                } else {
                    container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucune prescription trouvée.</p>';
                }
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('prescriptionsContainer').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger">Erreur chargement.</p>';
            }
        }

        chargerPrescriptions();
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    async function chargerSpecialistes() {
        try {
            const response = await fetch('/api/specialistes');
            const specialistes = await response.json();
            const container = document.getElementById('specialistesList');
            if (specialistes.length) {
                container.innerHTML = specialistes.map(s => `
                    <div class="col-md-4 mb-4">
                        <div class="card h-100 shadow-sm">

                                <p class="card-text"><strong>Spécialité :</strong> ${s.specialite}</p>
                                <p class="card-text"><strong>Tél :</strong> ${s.telephone || 'Non renseigné'}</p>
                                <p class="card-text"><strong>Email :</strong> ${s.email || 'Non renseigné'}</p>
                                <p class="card-text">${s.description || ''}</p>
                                ${s.cv_url ? `<a href="${s.cv_url}" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" target="_blank">Voir le CV</a>` : ''}
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                `).join('');
            } else {
                container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-center">Aucun spécialiste trouvé.</p>';
            }
        } catch (e) {
            document.getElementById('specialistesList').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger text-center">Erreur chargement.</p>';
        }
    }
    chargerSpecialistes();

    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mb-3">

        <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="window.location.href='ajout-course.html'">
            <i class="fas fa-plus"></i> Nouvelle course
        </button>
    </div>

    <div class="container-fluid px-4 py-4">
        <h2>Transferts du jour</h2>
        <div id="transfertsList" class="loading-container mt-4">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Chargement...</p>
        </div>

        <h2 class="mt-5">Véhicules disponibles</h2>
        <div id="vehiculesList" class="loading-container mt-4">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Chargement...</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        (async function () {
            try {
                // Récupération des courses
                const courses = await API.get('/courses');
                const transfertsContainer = document.getElementById('transfertsList');
                if (courses.length) {
                    transfertsContainer.innerHTML = courses.map(t => {
                        const date = new Date(t.date_depart);
                        const heure = date.toLocaleTimeString('fr-FR', { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
                        return `
                            <div class="consultation-card mb-2" style="border-left-color: #3498db;">
                                <strong>${heure}</strong> – ${t.patient_nom} ${t.patient_prenom}<br>
                                ${t.lieu_depart} → ${t.destination}<br>
                                Chauffeur : ${t.chauffeur_prenom} ${t.chauffeur_nom}<br>
                                Véhicule : ${t.immatriculation}<br>
                                <span class="badge-custom badge-${t.statut === 'terminee' ? 'success' : t.statut === 'en_cours' ? 'info' : 'warning'}">${t.statut}</span>
                            </div>
                        `;
                    }).join('');
                } else {
                    transfertsContainer.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucun transfert aujourd\'hui.</p>';
                }

                // Récupération des véhicules
                const vehicules = await API.get('/vehicules');
                const vehiculesContainer = document.getElementById('vehiculesList');
                if (vehicules.length) {
                    vehiculesContainer.innerHTML = vehicules.map(v => `
                        <div class="consultation-card mb-2" style="border-left-color: #3498db;">
                            <strong>${v.type}</strong> (${v.immatriculation})<br>
                            <span class="badge-custom badge-${v.etat === 'disponible' ? 'success' : v.etat === 'en_course' ? 'info' : 'danger'}">${v.etat}</span>
                        </div>
                    `).join('');
                } else {
                    vehiculesContainer.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted">Aucun véhicule trouvé.</p>';
                }

            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('transfertsList').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger">Erreur chargement.</p>';
            }
        })();
    </script>
</body>

</html>

        </div>
    </div>

        (async function () {
            try {
                const factures = [
                    { numero: "FAC-001", patient: "Mamadou Diop", montant: "49 500", statut: "payée" },
                    { numero: "FAC-002", patient: "Aminata Fall", montant: "27 500", statut: "en attente" },
                    { numero: "FAC-003", patient: "Ousmane Sow", montant: "137 500", statut: "impayée" },
                ];
                const container = document.getElementById('facturesList');
                container.innerHTML = factures.map(f => `
                <div class="consultation-card mb-2" style="border-left-color: #e74c3c;">
                <strong>${f.numero}</strong> – ${f.patient}<br>
                ${f.montant} DA<br>
                <span class="badge-custom badge-${f.statut === 'payée' ? 'success' : f.statut === 'en attente' ? 'warning' : 'danger'}">${f.statut}</span>
                </div>
            `).join('');
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('facturesList').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger">Erreur chargement.</p>';

=== FICHIER: js\api.js ===
// frontend/js/api.js
const API = {
    baseURL: 'https://clinique-hoteliere-et-actions.onrender.com/api',

    getToken() {
        return localStorage.getItem('token');
    },

    getHeaders() {
        const token = this.getToken();
        return {
            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            ...(token && { 'Authorization': `Bearer ${token}` })
        };
    },

    async get(endpoint) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseURL}${endpoint}`, {
                headers: this.getHeaders()
            });
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('❌ API GET Error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    },

    async post(endpoint, data) {
        try {
            const response = await fetch(`${this.baseURL}${endpoint}`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: this.getHeaders(),
                body: JSON.stringify(data)
            });
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);
            return await response.json();
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('❌ API POST Error:', error);
            throw error;
        }
    },

    // Récupérer les consultations d'un médecin
    async getConsultations(medecinId) {
        return this.get(`/consultations?medecin_id=${medecinId}`);
    },

    // Récupérer les patients
    async getPatients() {
        return this.get('/beneficiaires');
    },

    // Récupérer les rendez-vous
    async getRendezVous() {
        return this.get('/rendez-vous');
    },

    // Récupérer les statistiques
    async getStats() {
        return this.get('/statistiques/dashboard');
    },

    // Récupérer les constantes d'un patient
    async getConstantes() {
        return this.get('/constantes');
    },

    // Récupérer les stocks
    async getStocks() {
        return this.get('/stocks');
    },

    // Récupérer les indicateurs qualité
    async getQualite() {
        return this.get('/qualite/indicateurs');
    },

    // Récupérer les factures
    async getFactures() {
        return this.get('/factures');
    },

    // Déconnexion
    logout() {
        localStorage.removeItem('token');
        localStorage.removeItem('user');
        window.location.href = 'index.html';
    },

    // Récupérer l'utilisateur connecté
    getUser() {
        const user = localStorage.getItem('user');
        return user ? JSON.parse(user) : null;
    },

    setUser(user) {
        localStorage.setItem('user', JSON.stringify(user));
    }
};

<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="fr">

<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Consultations - Médecin</title>
    <link href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.3.0/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css" rel="stylesheet">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/font-awesome/6.0.0/css/all.min.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="../css/style.css">
    <script src="../js/api.js"></script>
</head>

<body>
    <nav class="navbar-custom" style="background: #3498db;">
        <div class="container-fluid px-4">
            <span class="navbar-brand"><i class="fas fa-stethoscope"></i> Consultations</span>
            <button class="btn btn-light btn-sm"
                onclick="window.location.href='../dashboard-medecin.html'">Retour</button>
        </div>
    </nav>

    <div class="container-fluid px-4 py-4">
        <h2>Liste des consultations</h2>
        <div id="consultationsList" class="loading-container mt-4">
            <div class="loading-spinner"></div>
            <p>Chargement...</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        (async function () {
            try {
                // Pour l'exemple, on appelle l'API pour 3 consultations (ids 1,2,3)
                const ids = [1, 2];
                const consultations = await Promise.all(ids.map(id => API.get(`/consultations/details/${id}`)));

                const container = document.getElementById('consultationsList');
                container.innerHTML = consultations.map(c => `
                 <div class="consultation-card mb-2">
                 <strong>${c.nom} ${c.prenom}</strong><br>
                 Date : ${c.date_heure}<br>
                 Motif : ${c.motif}<br>
                 Statut : ${c.statut}
                 </div>
                `).join('');
            } catch (e) {
                document.getElementById('consultationsList').innerHTML = '<p class="text-danger">Erreur chargement.</p>';
            }
        })();
    </script>
</body>

</html>
